  20. I assumed this would be a nice razor, I just didn't think it would be this good.<br /><br />Packaging:<br />The first thing you notice is that this razor is severely over packaged. First is the main box, which has two hefty seals that require a sharp object to cut them. Inside is a plastic clamshell containing the razor and the anti-theft devices. A sharp object is also needed to open this. Next is the big box that has the stand (wrapped in foam), cleaning brush, power adapter (one end wrapped in plastic), and the blade cover. Another box has the soft carrying case, which is in a plastic bag. Finally there is the box with a corrugated insert that contains the wash unit, which is wrapped in foam and in a plastic bag.<br /><br />First Impressions:<br />Nice touches abound. The cord for the adaptor has a Velcro wrap. The stand has suction cups on the bottom to keep it in place. The razor is nicely balanced. Everything has a quality feel to it. The manual is extensive, but for those who can't wait there is the \\"Quick Start\\" card...which is all pictures. Reading the fine print, I find it is made in the Netherlands, not China.<br /><br />Reading the Manual:<br />Sorry guys, I had to do it. The manual says it takes about 50 minutes to fully charge and you get about 50 minutes of shaving. It only charges in the stand or the wash unit. You cannot plug the razor in directly. If you let it run out, you can put it in the stand for 3-5 minutes and get 3-5 minutes of shaving. Norelco says not to leave the charger plugged in after charging fully, but doesn't say why. It has a neat LED \\"gas gauge\\" on the front to tell you the charge remaining.<br /><br />Like most electric razors, it says to use it for about four weeks to allow your face to \\"adjust\\" to it. Norelco gives you a 45 day money back guarantee as well as a two year warranty.<br /><br />When the battery will no longer hold a charge you have toss the razor...the battery is not replaceable. This is a huge negative in my opinion.<br /><br />Shaving:<br />I compared this razor to the [[ASIN:B001BJHCVO Remington Flex 360]] I tested earlier and to my old reliable blade, a Schick Quattro power. I shaved half my face with each and had a two- to three day growth each time.<br /><br />Norelco vs. Schick Quattro: I expected it to be no contest here, because everybody knows a blade shaves closer. The manual says I can use shaving cream with this razor, so I lather up with [[ASIN:B000RI8BZQ Proraso Shaving Cream]] using my trusty badger brush. Darned if it doesn't work! Just like with a manual blade, you have to rinse frequently, but it works great. The shave was very smooth, even against the grain, and much better than expected. There was a bit of irritation under the chin on the Norelco side. When done shaving, just open the rotary covers, rinse with hot water, and set in the stand to dry.<br /><br />The WifeTest: As is the norm in these shaving comparisons, I asked Mrs. Boilermate to judge which side is smoother. She said both sides were smooth, but, to my surprise, she said the Norelco side was \\"a bit smoother!\\" After two days I thought the Norelco side was a bit \\"skritchier\\" but Mrs. B, said there was no difference.<br /><br />Norelco vs. Remington: The Norelco feels more balanced than the Remington, which feels a bit top-heavy. The Norelco weighs in at 6.1 oz. vs 6.5 for the Remington. Both felt smooth and both irritated a bit under the chin. The Norelco's three separate heads make it easier to see what you are doing vs. the one big enclosure on the Remington. The individual heads allow you to get a bit closer, as well. The trimmers on each were easy to use, but the Norelco's is narrower and it sounds like something is loose when pressed against my face.<br /><br />Again, Mrs. B deemed the Norelco shave slightly better.<br /><br />Cleaning:<br />Both the Norelco and Remington rinse clean with hot water. To clean the Norelco, just open the three head covers and rinse with hot water and put in the stand with the heads open until dry. (It looks a bit like a Transformer in this mode!) The trimmer rinses clean as well.<br /><br />Every now and then you should run the razor thru the Jet Clean wash unit. The actual cleaning takes about five minutes, and about two hours to dry. It will charge the razor during the dry cycle. the manual gives instructions on how to disassemble the heads for cleaning as well.<br /><br />I prefer the Jet Clean system over the Braun's, mainly because the cleaning fluid is in a bottle instead of special refills. First of all, you get about two complete refills from a bottle for about the same price as one Braun refill. You can also empty the reservoir into another bottle and cap it between cleanings. That way it doesn't evaporate between cleanings and if you are short on counter space (as I am) you can put the wash unit in a drawer. I filter the fluid thru a coffee filter when reusing it. Norelco says you get about 15 cleanings per fill-up.<br /><br />Conclusion:<br />This thing is like a riding mower for your face...a John Deere, not one from WalMart, and that is a good thing. A good riding mower cuts as good as a good push mower but does it a lot faster. Yes, it cost more and requires a bit more maintenance, but to those who have one, it is all worth it.<br /><br />The price not withstanding, this is an awesome razor. It is well balanced and well built. It shaves as close as a blade, especially when used with shaving cream, and it covers a lot more territory so you are finished sooner. That being said, is it worth a nearly two hundred dollar premium over the Remington? Well, the Norelco comes with more: a stand, a carry case, and a cleaning system. So there is clearly added value. For the blade shaver who only occasionally uses an electric, it's hard to justify. If you use an electric regularly you can't go wrong with this one.<br /><br />UPDATE 1/13/11<br />Four months later and this razor has become my daily driver. I use it with shaving cream and get a quick smooth shave...even under the chin. And no more nicking the corners of my mouth trying to get close under my nose. After 40 years as a blade shaver I am a convert!<br /><br />UPDATE 9/11/12<br />It's been about two years since I first used this shaver and I'm still a convert. I primarily use it with [[ASIN:B002L03N74 Bigelow]] or [[ASIN:B00837ZOI0 Proraso]] shaving cream (rather than dry) and it gives a smooth, close shave. I just ordered a replacement head (Ouch! Fifty bucks!) because they say I should, but it is still doing a fantastic job. You can't go wrong with this shaver.

One places the razor upside down in this reservoir in a frame which holds the razor. Pressing the start button automatically begins the process. Eventually the process is finished when the razor is raised automatically to dry. It is comfortable, functional, easy to clean, and can be used wet or dry. If you're a (hairy) man, you're more than likely always trying to find the next best shaver, but hate to spend a fortune on one that may not do the job...<br /><br />Enter the Philips Norelco SensoTouch 3D Electric Shaver with Jet Clean System (black!). One hour will see your shaver from dead to full. Very nice. The instruction manual does recommend the shaver be removed from the charger when it is charged. I don't really know why, as most \\"intelligent\\" devices stop charging after the device is charged anyway to prevent overcharging and lessening battery life. I'm not sure what this Philips Norelco does in this regard, but again - it recommends removing the shaver from the charger when charged. I suspect it should be fine to leave it in the charger when you're done shaving.<br /><br />So how does it feel?<br /><br />Well, I have to say the first time you push the shaver against your dry face, it's like it's gently massaging your skin.... until you realize it's also removing hair at the same time. Woah! It's a really fun feeling, but it definitely takes a while to get your entire face shaved depending on how much stubble you have there. I won't lie - it's the absolute closest to a razor I've ever experienced from an electric. It really gets that close if you spend the time to be careful!<br /><br />That's not say it's perfect. I definitely rubbed my face a little too much in the process the first time, and I did feel a tad sore at the end, but I suspect this will ease with time. In fact, the manual suggests you use ONLY this shaver for 3 weeks so that your face can get used to it. I'll update this review in a few more weeks!<br /><br />When you're done with your shave, you can use the Jet Clean System, which I think is super cool. You fill (the first time) or empty+fill (subsequent times) the little tray in the bigger charging unit up to the marked line once every two weeks (if you use the shaver every day), and then when you're done shaving, you stick the shaver's head upside down into the Jet Clean System, hit the power button, and then the shaver automatically dunks itself into the liquid/foam/lubricant, runs some on/off clean cycles, and then lets itself dry over the course of two hours. Slick-looking device<br />2.) Not too noisy<br />3.) Not too much hair debris everywhere at all - surprised by this!<br />4.) Very fancy-looking charging LEDs on the shaver itself<br />5.) Very fancy magnets hold the shaver in place when it charges<br />6.) Has a nifty slide-out trimmer for below your nose or straightening out your sideburns<br />7.) Comes with a nice, zipped carrying case for traveling with your state-of-the-art shaver!<br />8.) Visual indicator when you need to replace the shaving heads<br />9.) Two-year warranty<br /><br />Cons:<br /><br />1.) Definitely will take a bit of an adjustment period if your skin isn't used to such a close shave<br />2.) The mini-charger doesn't take up a huge amount of room, but the Jet Clean System is definitely not something that could be called subtle... so plan accordingly!<br />3.) When using the slide out trimmer, it can be tricky to see whereyou're trimming with the shaving blades in the way<br />4.) Have to buy Philips Norelco's special cleaning/lubricating liquid for the Jet Clean System<br />5.) Non-replaceable battery<br />6.) Or, shave, rinse well and place in the Jet Clean System, turn on, and let it do its thing. *TIP* You can turn off the Jet Cleaner because the charger still works as long as the SensoTouch is in the Cleaning System's cradle. *TIP 2* - If you get a Philips Norelco 1250xcc/42 SensoTouch 3d Electric Shaver with the Jet Clean System, make sure you rinse it very well (before, during, and after) while shaving with foam, or a gel. But the price isn't just for the razor and believe me, the Philips Norelco 1250xcc/42 SensoTouch 3D would be a bargain at $189, without the Jet Clean System. But as it is, you get the Jet Clean System, a Recharging stand, and a nicely tailored travel case, plus your first bottle of cleaning solution for the Jet Clean System, which lasts far longer than many reviewers have implied. Bottom Line - Most men know what 'kind' of electric shave they feel best with. Some feel they get a better shave from a foil razor, others like the triple head shaver by Remington, or Norelco because their faces can't tell the difference. My face is sensitive, but I also have some white hairs that are hard to cut. If I use a foil razor, my face gets burned.   123. 35 years ago my Father told me \\"If Your going to use an electric razor - use a Braun\\" and so began a relationship with Braun products that up until recently has lasted close to forty years.<br /><br />What set Braun apart from every single other electric razor on the planet was it's Patented Optifoil. It was unlike anything else. Instead of uniform, same shaped holes. The foil had a wide variety of different shapes.<br /><br />Circles, half moons, crescents, stars and so on. It seemed random in placement but there was a method to the madness and you really ended up with a blade close shave.The foil and cutter (linear blades designed by Gillette) may be the head of the razor but when it comes to performance this is the very heart of any electric razor.<br /><br />Being both a head and face shaver, I prefer a wet shave with a DE (double edge) safety razor or straight blade. But the process is time consuming. I've tried other electrics over the years - including rotary razors which I never cared for and found them sub par on every level to the Braun.<br /><br />Enter Proctor & Gamble.<br /><br />When P&G bought Gillette and Braun they made significant changes. The small appliances division was closed down. Manufacturing of the electric razors was terminated in Germany and resumed in China with the exception of the 760 & 790cc which are still, at least for the time being made in Germany.<br /><br />What is more, P&G scrapped the original foil and replaced it with a generic one. Now with uniform octagon punch holes and without the center \\" Active Lift\\" strip this once excellent razor now shaves as well as any $40 piece of junk. (luckily I have one new original replacement left)<br /><br />Intrigued by the positive reviews as well the high rating on Consumer Reports I bought the new Norelco Sensotouch 3D 1250X and am delighted I did..<br /><br />At first the shave was rough and poor but I'm finding as time goes on each shave is noticeably faster, easier and cleaner. The look of the razor is sensational, sexy, sleek and wonderfully ergonomically designed. It's also without question the quitest electric razor I've ever used. It's surprisingly light, well balanced and fits nicely in the hand. The heads of the razor pivot so much and so effortlessly it's the perfect razor for head shavers such as myself.<br /><br />I find I get the closest shave by going with the grain in straight stroked as opposed to the suggested circular motions - but like any razor electric or not it's all very subjective and personal. The key is always to find out what works for you best.<br /><br />The Cleaning System<br /><br />The cleaning and charging system is the best I've seen. It's a marvel to watch, takes up very little space and does an excellent job. I use it after each shave, but that may change. For instance the little stand alone charger has small suction cups on the bottom to keep it in place, each of the three heads are effortless to open and shake clean. Build quality appears excellent. I definitely recommend this product. Don't press to hard let the razor do the work. Pull the face tight up at an angle to really get close, you will know when your done by the sound and the feel of the razor on your face. After wet shaving she said my face felt as smooth as a babies bottom, so did my 15 year old daughter. So at least she has stopped complaining about how much it cost especially after she found out some versions are twice as much. Anyway, my son was so impressed he ordered one from Amazon last week. Maybe I should get a cut! The biggest most impressive thing about it though was the next morning after wet shaving, my face was still pretty smooth. Normally by morning my stubble would be so rough and thick, but, my face felt great. The next day wet shaving with it felt even better and smoother. If you use a gel just wash your face good with hot water, leave it wet put a very light coat of gel and shave away. It works great and your face will thank you, so will your wife. We replaced it, and then that one broke too. Then we got the Braun Pulsonic -- slightly better shave, slightly better cleaning system -- it broke after about a year. And finally, we tried the Panasonic Arc 5. Seemed to be the best razor by a mile, which was good considering the VERY steep price. But then, after a couple weeks, the cleaning system started it fail; it never turned itself off and would go literally for hours on end if we didn't babysit it. Complete junk.<br /><br />Enter Phillips Norelco<br /><br />I'd used their original 3 head shaver many many moons ago, then was lost to Braun and Panasonic for years, before I finally found my way back here. I have to say, in the years since my absence form this product, they've really upped the anti. This is without question, the best razor I've ever owned! The 3D technology is no joke -- it really does make a difference in shave quality. Each head floats independently across my face for a near flawless shave, each and every time. Unlike my other shavers that caused razor burn, I don't have to press this Norelco hard to my face. It just gently glides across my face, easily mowing down all the whiskers in its path. Best shave ever by far. Fast and easy too.<br /><br />Excellent Cleaning Base<br /><br />It's like putting your razor into a little Jacuzzi bath all its own. The motorized mechanics precisely lower the razor into its little bath, and then get it all shiny and squeaky clean. It does a great job and looks really cool and cutting edge too. Oh, and best of all, it's QUIET!!! My Braun's always sounded like a Learjet was taking off in my bathroom! No joke! But this Norelco is smooth as silk; quiet, effective, and economical to operate. Unlike Braun, that was overly expensive for their cleaning solution, this Norelco is very affordable at barely four bucks a bottle. Better still, it's more readily available locally than the Braun solution ever was. And the Norelco seems to last a good while, so I won't be spending as much and can clean my razor more often since it's economical.<br /><br />***Helpful Tip*** - Definitely get the frustration free packaging!
